BASIC OAKLAND ARTCC ON VATSIM CONTROLLERS ALIAS LIST
Amendments by Chuck Barlow, Charan Kumar, Jon O'Malley, Dominic Nguyen, Ryan Parry, Jackson Gilliam, Rowan Young
February 24, 2022
AIRAC 2202

GENERAL
.gm Good morning
.ga Good afternoon
.ge Good evening
.y Affirmative
.n Negative
.thx Thank you
.sa Say again

.airmet .openurl http://aviationweather.gov/adds/airmets/

.checksq Check your squawk code, squawk $squawk.
.sqn Squawk normal / Mode C
.id Ident.
.sqi Squawk $squawk and ident.
.sq Squawk $squawk.
.rsq Reset transponder, squawk $squawk.
.sqt sq $squawk
.alt $1 Altimeter $altim($1)
.depalt $dep altimeter $altim($dep)
.arralt $arr altimeter $altim($arr)

.me $metar($1)
.depme $metar($dep)
.arrme $metar($arr)

.depcharts All current departure procedures for $dep can be found on www.airnav.com/airport/$dep
.arrcharts All current arrival procedures and instrument approaches for $arr can be found on www.airnav.com/airport/$arr

.ho Contact $atccallsign($1) on $freq($1)
.noatc No further ATC is available, monitor UNICOM on 122.80, have a good day.

.po .msg $radioname($1) Pointout, $dist($2) miles $bear($2) of $2, $aircraft at $calt
.poa .msg $radioname($1) Pointout approved, $2

.fb .msg $aircraft To improve our services provided to you as a pilot, please be so kind and take a minute to provide feedback on $myrealname working $callsign at "https://oakartcc.org/pilots/feedback". Thank you for your assistance.

Pre Departure Clearances:

.pdc .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE  $dep $route $arr | *CLB VIA SID*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $1   PLAN RWY $uc($2) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION  

.pdcc .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE CHANGED  - $dep $route $arr - | *CLB VIA SID*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $1   PLAN RWY $uc($2) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION

.pdcx .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE  $dep $route $arr | *CLB VIA SID EXC MAINT $1*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $2   PLAN RWY $uc($3) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION  

.pdcxc .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE CHANGED  - $dep $route $arr - | *CLB VIA SID EXC MAINT $1*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $2   PLAN RWY $uc($3) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION

.pdcm .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE  $dep $route $arr | *MAINTAIN $1*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $2   PLAN RWY $uc($3) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION 

.pdcmc .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** $aircraft   DEPART $dep   AT $ftime(30)Z   $cruise | $type($aircraft)    TRANSPONDER $squawk | ROUTE CHANGED  - $dep $route $arr - | *MAINTAIN $1*   EXP $cruise 10 MIN AFT DP DPFRQ $2   PLAN RWY $uc($3) ATC MAY CHANGE ANY TIME   RESPOND ACCEPT OR CTC $freq() FOR REVISION

.nopdc .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** PRE-DEPARTURE CLEARANCE UNAVAILABLE. CTC $freq($1) FOR CLEARANCE.

.pdcgh .msg $aircraft **** PREDEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE **** GATE HOLD PROCEDURES IN EFFECT.  CONTACT $radioname($1) ON $freq($1) WHEN READY FOR PUSHBACK AND START.

.pdcend .msg $aircraft - ADDITIONAL INFORMATION: PUSH AND START AT YOUR DISCRETION. EXPECT RUNWAY $1 FOR DEPARTURE. THIS MESSAGE SERVES AS YOUR PRE-DEPARTURE CLEARANCE. YOU DO NOT NEED TO REPLY TO THIS MESSAGE. CONTACT CLEARANCE DELIVERY ONLY IF YOU HAVE QUESTIONS REGARDING YOUR CLEARANCE. **DEPARTURE CLEARANCE END** 
 
.pdcendp .msg $aircraft - ADDITIONAL INFORMATION: CONTACT $radioname($1) ON $freq($1) FOR PUSH AND START CLEARANCE. EXPECT RUNWAY $2 FOR DEPARTURE. THIS MESSAGE SERVES AS YOUR PRE-DEPARTURE CLEARANCE. YOU DO NOT NEED TO REPLY TO THIS MESSAGE. CONTACT CLEARANCE DELIVERY ONLY IF YOU HAVE QUESTIONS REGARDING YOUR CLEARANCE. **DEPARTURE CLEARANCE END**


CLEARANCE:
.cor clearance on request, standby...
.cor# clearance on request, standby, you are number $1 in sequence...
.pref preferred route to $arr is
.can - can you accept?
.preftec preferred route to $arr is $route - can you accept?

Clearance Questions:
.cua Can you accept the $1 departure?
.cuarv Can you accept the $1 departure, radar vectors $2, then as filed?
.cuatr Can you accept the $1 departure, $2 transition, then as filed?

Clearance Misc
.xfp I have no flightplan for you, please refile.
.wralt The altitude you filed is incorrect for your direction of flight, may I suggest $1 or $2?
.wrrte The route you filed is not the preferred route for this flight, may I suggest the following routing: $1
.dwx $dep wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep), METAR $metar($dep)
.dwxa $dep Information $1 current, wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep)
.dwxpm .msg $aircraft $dep wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep), METAR $metar($dep). Push and start your discretion
.dwxapm .msg $aircraft $dep Information $1 current, wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep). Push and start your discretion
.dwxp $dep wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep), METAR $metar($dep). Push and start your discretion
.dwxap $dep Information $1 current, wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep). Push and start your discretion
.awx $arr wind $wind($arr), altimeter $altim($arr). METAR $metar($arr)
.awxa $arr Information $1 current, wind $wind($arr), altimeter $altim($arr)
Cleared To:
.cdt cleared to $arr airport; $1 departure, $2 transition, then as filed;
.cd cleared to $arr airport; $1 departure, $2, then as filed;

.cdrv cleared to $arr airport via radar vectors to $1, then as filed;
.cdrw cleared to $arr airport; via fly runway heading, radar vectors to $1, then as filed;
.cdhg cleared to $arr airport; via fly heading $1, radar vectors to $2, then as filed;

.cdtd cleared to $arr airport; $1 departure, $2 transition, direct $arr airport;
.cdd cleared to $arr airport; $1 departure, $2, direct $arr airport;
.cdrwd cleared to $arr airport; via fly runway heading, radar vectors to $1, direct $arr airport;
.cdrvd cleared to $arr airport via radar vectors to $1, direct $arr airport;
.cdhgd cleared to $arr airport; via fly heading $1, radar vectors to $2, direct $arr airport;

.cdf cleared to $arr airport; $1 departure, $2 transition, $3 arrival;
.cfiled cleared to $arr airport as filed;

Clearance Altitude:
.calt maintain 5,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.calt10 maintain 10,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.calt15 maintain 15,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.calt19 maintain FL190, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk

.caltu maintain 5,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.calt10u maintain 10,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.calt15u maintain 15,000, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.calt19u maintain FL190, expect $cruise 10 minutes after departure, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk

Climb Via SID:
.cvs climb via SID, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.cvs5 climb via SID except maintain 5,000, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.cvs10 climb via SID except maintain 10,0000, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.cvs15 climb via SID except maintain 15,000, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk
.cvs19 climb via SID except maintain FL190, departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk

.cvsu climb via SID, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.cvs5u climb via SID except maintain 5,000, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.cvs10u climb via SID except maintain 10,0000, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.cvs15u climb via SID except maintain 15,000, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk
.cvs19u climb via SID except maintain FL190, departure’s not online, squawk $squawk

Clearance Readback
.rbc Readback correct, $dep wind $wind($dep), altimeter $altim($dep), expect runway $1 for departure, advise ready to taxi.

GROUND:

Taxi instructions:
.txv Runway $uc($1), taxi via $uc($2) $uc($3) $uc($4) $uc($5) $uc($6) $uc($7)
.txp Taxi to the ramp via $uc($1), See ya!
.gav Taxi to the general aviation parking via $uc($1)
.hs hold short runway $uc($1).

SFO Shortcuts:
.1r Runway 1R, taxi via A, A1
.1l Runway 1L, taxi via A, M1
.28l Runway 28L, taxi via A, F, hold short runway 1L.
.28R Runway 28R, taxi via A, F, C, hold short runway 1L.

S2 ALIAS COMMANDS

Tower Take Off:
.to Wind $winds, runway $1, cleared for takeoff.
.tor RNAV to $1, wind $winds, runway $2, cleared for takeoff
.frh Fly runway heading.
.luaw Runway $1, line-up and wait.
.tomlt Wind $winds, make left closed traffic, runway $1, cleared for takeoff.
.tomrt Wind $winds, make right closed traffic, runway $1, cleared for takeoff.

Tower Landing:
.land Wind $winds, runway $1, cleared to land.
.ga Go around.

Tower VFR: 
.coption Wind $winds, runway $1, cleared for the option.
.msi Make straight in runway $1, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).
.elb Enter left base runway $1, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).
.erb Enter right base runway $1, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).
.eld Enter left downwind runway $1, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).
.erd Enter right downwind runway $1, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).

.mlt Make left traffic
.mrt Make right traffic
.ml3 Make a left 360.
.mr3 Make a right 360.

.extuw Extend your upwind leg, I will call your crosswind turn.
.extdw Extend your downwind leg, I will call your base turn.

Tower General:
.cjb Caution, jet blast.
.cwt Caution, wake turbulence.
.thip Traffic holding in position runway $1.
.tlr Traffic landing runway $1.
.wel Welcome to $arr airport, exit left when able.
.wer Welcome to $arr airport, exit right when able.
.ctc Contact $radioname($1)on $freq($1) Good day.

Tower Weather:
.newatis Attention all aircraft, $1 ATIS information $atiscode now current, wind $wind($1), altimeter $altim($1).

.B2D .autotrack KMRY KSNS KSJC KNUQ KPAO KRHV KMOD KMER KSCK KLVK KHWD KSFO KOAK KSMF KSAC KMHR KBAB
.C2D .autotrack KMRY KSNS KSJC KNUQ KPAO KRHV KSQL KSFO KOAK KSMF KSAC KMHR KBAB
.D2D .autotrack KMRY KSNS KSJC KNUQ KPAO KRHV KSQL KMOD KMER KSCK KLVK KHWD KSMF KSAC KMHR KBAB

.R2D .autotrack KRNO
.DAY .autotrack KMRY KSNS KSJC KNUQ KPAO KRHV KSQL KMOD KMER KSCK KLVK KHWD KSFO KOAK KSMF KSAC KMHR KBAB
.ALL .autotrack KMRY KSNS KSJC KNUQ KPAO KRHV KSQL KMOD KMER KSCK KLVK KHWD KSFO KOAK KSMF KSAC KMHR KBAB KRNO KRTS KFAT KFCH KVIS KRDD KRBL KSUU KTVL KSTS KUKI
.RB .autotrack NONE
.gd .asdex $1
.assc .asdex $1
.tvis .vis KMRY KRNO KMCE SAU

.rc radar contact
.rccm radar contact, climb and maintain $uc($1)
.rcsalt radar contact, say altitude
.rcvfr radar contact, maintain VFR
.rcl radar contact lost

.rcp radar contact $dist($1) miles $bear($1) of $uc($1)
.rcpcm radar contact $dist($1) miles $bear($1) of $uc($1), climb and maintain $2
.rcpsalt radar contact $dist($1) miles $bear($1) of $uc($1), $arr altimeter $altim($arr), say altitude
.rcpsfl radar contact $dist($1) miles $bear($1) of $uc($1), say flight level

.fhdct Fly heading $1, when able proceed direct $2, resume own navigation.
.cdct Cleared direct $1, resume own navigation.
.dct Proceed direct $1.
.ron Resume own navigation.

.cv climb via SID 
.cvxm climb via SID except maintain $1
.cvxa climb via SID except cross $uc($1) at or above $2
.cvxb climb via SID except cross $uc($1) at or below $2

.cm Climb and maintain $1.
.dm Descend and maintain $1.
.dpd Descend at pilots discretion, maintain $1.
.aftdm After $1 descend and maintain $2.
.xalt Cross $1 at and maintain $2.
.dscv Descend via the $1 arrival, $arr altimeter $altim($arr).

.exapp Expect $1 runway $2 approach.

.tr Turn right heading $1.
.tl Turn left heading $1.
.fh Fly heading $1.
.fixhdg Depart $1 heading $2.
.cdct Cleared direct $1, resume own navigation.
.vecapp Vectors for the approach.
.vecv Vector visual approach to $1.

.mspd Maintain $1 knots.
.rspd Reduce speed to $1.
.ispd Increase speed to $1.

.ptacl $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), turn left heading $2, maintain $3 until established on the localizer, cleared $4 runway $5 approach
.ptacr $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), turn right heading $2, maintain $3 until established on the localizer, cleared $4 runway $5 approach
.locptac $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), fly heading $2, maintain $3 until established on the localizer, cleared $4 runway $5 approach.
.bcptac $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), fly heading $2, maintain $3 until established on the localizer backcourse, cleared localizer backcourse runway $4 approach.
.npptac $dist($1) miles from $uc($1), fly heading $2, maintain $3 until established on the final approach course, cleared $4 runway $5 approach.

.vapp The $arr airport is at your $oclock($arr) and $dist($arr) miles, report the airport in sight.
.cvapp Cleared visual approach runway $1

.iafclr Cleared direct $1, cross $1 at or above $2, cleared $3 runway $4 approach
.aiafclr  Cross $1 at or above $2, cleared $3 runway $4 approach

.sap When able, select approach to $arr.

.rel Released for departure, clearance void if not off by $ftime(5)Z. If not off by $ftime(5)Z, advise $callsign no later than $ftime(8)Z of intentions, time now $timeZ. Report airborne this frequency, change to advisory frequency approved
.hfr Hold for release, remain this frequency
.notr No traffic observed between you and the $arr airport, radar service terminated, report IFR cancellation this frequency, change to advisory frequency approved.


.fma Fly the missed approach procedure as published

.leavingb Leaving San Francisco Bravo airspace. Radar service is terminated, squawk 1200, frequency change approved. Good day.
.leavingc Leaving Charlie airspace. Radar service is terminated, squawk 1200, frequency change approved. Good day.

ZAK commands
INITIAL CONTACTS
.con Position reports consist of - Last crossed fix and time crossed, altitude, next fix and estimated time of crossing, next fix after that, mach, ground speed
.hi Hello. Pass me the time at which you crossed your last waypoint, flight level, estimate for your next waypoint, name of waypoint after that, mach number and groundspeed
.call $1 Hello, when you get a chance, please contact me on $freq($1)
.callpos Hello, please contact me on $freq() over your NEXT waypoint, for a FULL position report

ROUTING
.nodctgps I'm sorry, but DCT GPS is not a quite preffered routing
.flun FL$1 is NOT available,
.r Are you routing via an Airway, a random oceanic routing or a completely non-oceanic routing?
.cm Climb and maintain $1
.dm Descend and maintain $1
.ra report at $1

POSITION REPORTS
.pos For your position report, please pass the time at which you have crossed $1, your flight level, your estimate in Zulu for $2, the name of the waypoint after that, your mach number and your groundspeed
.check $radioname() copies $1 at $2, flight level $3, Estimating $4 at $5, $6 next, Mach $7, Groundspeed $8
.rest wind $1, OAT $2, fuel $3
.rnwtf Report next waypoint this frequency
.rnwf Report next waypoint frequency $freq($1)
.rnptf Report next position this frequency
.rnptf@ Report next position this frequency, at $1 ZULU
.rnpf Report next position frequency $freq($1)
.rnpf@ Report next position frequency $freq($1), at $2 ZULU

HANDOFF
.ho contact $radioname($1), $freq($1), have a good flight, so long
.chad change to advisory frequency approved, so long
.lma leaving my airspace, frequency change approved, so long

MISCELLANEOUS
.brb All aircraft $radioname() will be right back
.bk All aircraft $radioname() is back
.closing **NOTAM** $radioname() is closing in $1 minute(s)
.closed **NOTAM** $radioname() is closed, thanks for flying
.closedho **NOTAM** $radioname() is closed, make further requests with $radioname($1) on $freq($1), thanks for flying
.closedu **NOTAM** $radioname() is closed, change to advisory frequency approved, thanks for flying
.ownnav This is an oceanic radio station, I cannot provide any domestic ATC in your area. Change to advisory frequency approved, have a good flight, so long
.zakvis .vis ZAGER CINTO CROBY FFVIS

.o .msg $1 *** $2
.gen General reminder to all planes to squwak 2000 while within Oakland Oceanic FIR

HOLDS:
.phold Cleared direct $1, hold as published, expect further clearance $ftime($2) Zulu.
.hold Cleared direct $1, hold $2 of $1 on $1-$3 radial $4, $5 turns, $6 minute legs, expect further clearance $ftime($7) Zulu.

BAD PILTOS:
.BADRWY1 .msg $aircraft Hello, you have started up on an active runway, please disconnect immediately and relocate your aircraft to the nearest ramp. Do not slew or taxi. Thank you. 

.BADTWY1 .msg $aircraft Hello, you have started up on an active taxiway, please relocate your aircraft to the nearest ramp immediately. Do not slew or taxi. Thank you. 

.BADPUSH1 .msg $aircraft Hello, please be observant of online ATC next time prior to pushing back from the gate and/or taxiing. Thank you. 

.BADRWY Hello, you have started up on an active runway, please disconnect immediately and relocate your aircraft to the nearest ramp. Do not slew or taxi. Thank you. 

.BADTWY Hello, you have started up on an active taxiway, please relocate your aircraft to the nearest ramp immediately. Do not slew or taxi. Thank you. 

.BADPUSH Hello, please be observant of online ATC next time prior to pushing back from the gate and/or taxiing. Thank you. 
.PRC In order to better your flying experience and skill, please visit the VATSIM Pilot Resource Center at http://www.vatsim.net/prc

.PRCNEW Welcome to VATSIM! In order to have a better understanding of the basics, and to know what is required of you as pilot, please visit the VATSIM Pilot Resource Center at http://www.vatsim.net/prc.

.PRCBUSY While I would love to answer your questions and help you become familiar with the VATSIM environment, my work load is quite large at this time. Please visit the Pilot Resource Center located at http://wwww.vatsim.net/prc. We hope to see you back after you have a better understanding of what is required as a pilot on VATSIM.

Tower Coordination:
.tcord .msg $atccallsign($1) ***  $dep $aircraft $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $alt
.RL .msg $atccallsign($1) $aircraft Rolling $2, $3 SID
.RLRV .msg $atccallsign($1) $aircraft Rolling $2, Radar Vectors.
.rd .msg $atccallsign($1) ***  $dep $aircraft $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $alt

Terminal Coordination:
.fatscratch .msg FAT_SCH *** ENTRY | DEFINITION ::: SIS | Straight-in SFO :::::: FR1 | IFR approach going to Friant Radar :::::: GPR | GPS 29R/11R :::::: GPL | GPS 29L/11L :::::: HR1 | IFR approach going to HR :::::: LOC | Localizer approach to 11L :::::: ILS | ILS approach to 29R :::::: PTN | IFR approach stay VFR with tower :::::: BRK | Overhead Break :::::: 11L | Class C arrival 11L ::::::  29L | Class C arrival 29L ::::::  VOR | VOR 11L ::::::  OTP | On Top ::::::  11R | Class C arrival 11R :::::: 29R | Class C arrival 29R :::::: SFO | Simulated flameout :::::: SVF | Special VFR :::::: VAR | VA or CTC to 11R or 29R :::::: VAL | VA or CTC to 11L or 29L :::
.nctscratch .msg NCT_SCH *** ENTRY | DEFINITION ::: BTR | Aircraft requesting the Bayshore Transition :::::: CTR | Aircraft requesting the Coastline Transition :::::: NEF | Aircraft on the Northeast Bay Flyway :::::: NWF | Aircraft on the Northwest Bay Flyway :::::: PTR | Aircraft requesting the Pacifica Transition :::::: SEF | Aircraft on the Southeast Bay Flyway :::::: SWF | Aircraft on the Southwest Bay Flyway :::::: T## | Aircraft is on a T-Route. ## is last 2 digits of the T-Route.(e.g., T329 is ?T39) :::::: 2ER | Aircraft sight-seeing in the San Francisco Bay Area :::::: AIS | Airport in sight ::::::  BNR | Banner Tow ::::::  BVA | Aircraft cleared for visual approach via bayside ::::::  GPS | Aircraft requesting/assigned a GPS approach to advertised runway ::::::  H## | Assigned heading followed by a two-digit number :::::: III | Coordination of Category 3 ILS approach :::::: ILS | Aircraft requesting/assigned an ILS approach to advertised runway :::::: 1MP/2MP | Coordination for Parachute Jump Aircraft within 2 minutes of releasing parachutists :::::: ##K | Aircraft assigned a speed in knots :::::: LOC | Aircraft requesting/assigned a LOC approach to advertised runway :::::: OPN | Operational law enforcement. :::::: PIX | Photo Mission. :::::: R## | Specific runway request ::::::  RNV | Aircraft requesting/assigned a RNAV approach to advertised runway :::::: RVA | Aircraft requesting a visual approach :::::: SVR | Special VFR :::::: TFC | Aircraft providing automobile traffic reporting :::::: V## | RVR landing value required by aircraft in hundreds of feet ::::::  V2I | VFR aircraft requesting an IFR clearance airborne and has IFR flight plan on file exiting NCT airspace. ::::::  VA | Aircraft cleared for a visual approach. ::::::  VOR | Aircraft requesting/assigned a VOR approach to advertised runway :::::: Single Letter | Singgle with no other info indicates ATIS code last reported by pilot for landing airport :::
